However,\\n21: `x` cannot be moved because the borrow to `_ref_to_val`\\n22: needs to last till the function `borrow`.\\n23: To fix that you can do a few different things:\\n24: \\n25: * Try to avoid moving the variable.\\n26: * Release borrow before move.\\n27: * Implement the `Copy` trait on the type.\\n28: \\n29: Examples:\\n30: \\n31: ```\\n32: struct Value {}\\n33: \\n34: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\\n35: \\n36: fn eat(val: &Value) {}\\n37: \\n38: fn main() {\\n39:     let x = Value{};\\n40: \\n41:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\\n42:     eat(&x); // pass by reference, if it's possible\\n43:     borrow(ref_to_val);\\n44: }\\n45: ```\\n46: \\n47: Or:\\n48: \\n49: ```\\n50: struct Value {}\\n51: \\n52: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\\n53: \\n54: fn eat(val: Value) {}\\n55: \\n56: fn main() {\\n57:     let x = Value{};\\n58: \\n59:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\\n60:     borrow(ref_to_val);\\n61:     // ref_to_val is no longer used.\\n62:     eat(x);\\n63: }\\n64: ```\\n65: \\n66: Or:\\n67: \\n68: ```\\n69: #[derive(Clone, Copy)] // implement Copy trait\\n70: struct Value {}\\n71: \\n72: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\\n73: \\n74: fn eat(val: Value) {}\\n75: \\n76: fn main() {\\n77:     let x = Value{};\\n78:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\\n79:     eat(x); However,\\n21: `x` cannot be moved because the borrow to `_ref_to_val`\\n22: needs to last till the function `borrow`.\\n23: To fix that you can do a few different things:\\n24: \\n25: * Try to avoid moving the variable.\\n26: * Release borrow before move.\\n27: * Implement the `Copy` trait on the type.\\n28: \\n29: Examples:\\n30: \\n31: ```\\n32: struct Value {}\\n33: \\n34: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\\n35: \\n36: fn eat(val: &Value) {}\\n37: \\n38: fn main() {\\n39:     let x = Value{};\\n40: \\n41:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\\n42:     eat(&x); However,\n21: `x` cannot be moved because the borrow to `_ref_to_val`\n22: needs to last till the function `borrow`.\n23: To fix that you can do a few different things:\n24: \n25: * Try to avoid moving the variable.\n26: * Release borrow before move.\n27: * Implement the `Copy` trait on the type.\n28: \n29: Examples:\n30: \n31: ```\n32: struct Value {}\n33: \n34: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n35: \n36: fn eat(val: &Value) {}\n37: \n38: fn main() {\n39:     let x = Value{};\n40: \n41:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n42:     eat(&x); // pass by reference, if it's possible\n43:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n44: }\n45: ```\n46: \n47: Or:\n48: \n49: ```\n50: struct Value {}\n51: \n52: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n53: \n54: fn eat(val: Value) {}\n55: \n56: fn main() {\n57:     let x = Value{};\n58: \n59:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n60:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n61:     // ref_to_val is no longer used.\n62:     eat(x);\n63: }\n64: ```\n65: \n66: Or:\n67: \n68: ```\n69: #[derive(Clone, Copy)] // implement Copy trait\n70: struct Value {}\n71: \n72: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n73: \n74: fn eat(val: Value) {}\n75: \n76: fn main() {\n77:     let x = Value{};\n78:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n79:     eat(x); // it will be copied here.\n80:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n81: }\n82: ```\n83: \n84: For more information on Rust's ownership system, take a look at the\n85: [References & Borrowing][references-and-borrowing] section of the Book.\n86: \n87: [references-and-borrowing]: https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-02-references-and-borrowing.html\n88: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/rust--01f6ddf7@525258043d7f9dcc1b69d9abcb9bfea32826a219/-/blob/compiler/rustc_error_codes/src/error_codes/E0505.md"}}}
